// Java Code von Gamification 1 Mathe für Informatiker und Matrixgame, KI-Game und Luminii Zahlen und Mathematik und Translate Traininig und Mehr:
package p1;

import java.util.Arrays;

import acm.program.DialogProgram;
import acm.program.GraphicsProgram;

public class MatheFuerInformatiker extends DialogProgram {
	/**
	 * PartyTest Created on Mar 14, 2015
	 * 
	 * @author Andreas
	 */
	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;

	String[][] score = new String[20][2];
	int level = 1;
	double richtig = 0;
	int start = 0;
	int sicher = 0;
	int[] q = new int[50];
	long bonuszeit = 0;
	
	int consecutiveErrors=0;

	
	
	
	public void run() {
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(0));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(1));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(2));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(3));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(4));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(5));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(6));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(7));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(8));
		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(9));
		
		System.out.println("zahln");
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("0",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("1",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("00",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("01",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("10",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("11",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("000",2));
		System.out.println(newLuminiNumberToDecimal("001",2));
//		System.out.println(longToNewLumini(5));
		
		
		
		long zeitbegrenzung = 60000 + bonuszeit;
		long sekunden = zeitbegrenzung / 1000;
		int counter = 0;
		long zeitAfter = 0;
		while (start != 1) {
			if (start == 3)
				sicher = readInt("Wirklich beenden?\n1 = Ja, 2 = Nein\n");
			if (start == 3 && sicher == 1)
				exit();
			if (start == 2)
				showHighscore();
			start = readInt("1 = Start, 2 = Highscore, 3 = Ende\n");
		}
		println("Level " + level + " (Zeitbegrenzung = " + sekunden + "s)");

		long zeitBefore = System.currentTimeMillis();
		long zeit = 0;
		while (counter < 10) {
			zeitAfter = System.currentTimeMillis();
			zeit = zeitAfter - zeitBefore;
			if (zeit > zeitbegrenzung) {
				println("Zeitüberschreitung!");
				break;
			}
			int frage = (int) (Math.random() * 50);
			if (frage == 0 && Math.random() > 0.9)
				for (int i = 0; i < q.length; i++)
					q[i] = 0;
			if (frage == 1 && q[1] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " * " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 * x2)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x2 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[1] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 37 && q[37] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " x " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x(x1,x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x(x1,x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[37] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
			if (frage == 38 && q[38] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x3 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " * " + x2 + " * "+x3 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 * x2 * x3)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x2 * x3 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[38] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
			
			
			if (frage == 39 && q[39] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x3 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " x " + "("+x2 + " * "+x3 +")"+ "\n");
				if (a == x(x1,x2*x3))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x(x1,x2*x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[39] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
			if (frage == 40 && q[40] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x3 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " * "  +"("+x2 + " x "+x3 +")"+ "\n");
				if (a == x1 * x(x2,x3))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x(x2,x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[40] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 41 && q[41] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int x3 = (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (3 + 2 * level)));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " x " + x2 + " x "+x3 + "\n");
				if (a == x(x(x1,x2),x3))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x(x(x1,x2),x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[41] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 2 && q[2] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (8 + 2 * level));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level)) * x1;
				int a = readInt(x2 + " / " + x1 + "\n");
				if (a == x2 / x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x2 / x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[2] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 3 && q[3] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(2, level));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " + " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 + x2)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + (x1 + x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[3] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 4 && q[4] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(2, level));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " - " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 - x2)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + (x1 - x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[4] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 5 && q[5] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 5);
				int a = readInt(x1 + " ^ " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == Math.pow(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Math.pow(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[5] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 6 && q[6] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level));
				int x2 = 2 + (int) (Math.random() * 3);
				int a = readInt((int) Math.pow(x1, x2) + " ^ " + "1/" + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[6] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 7 && q[7] == 0) {
				int x1 = 2;
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " ^ " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == Math.pow(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Math.pow(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[7] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
			if (frage == 42 && q[42] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 5);
				int a = readInt(x1 + " hoch " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == hoch(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + hoch(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[42] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 43 && q[43] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = 2 + (int) (Math.random() * 3);
				int a = readInt((int) hoch(x1, x2) + " hoch " + "1/" + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[43] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 44 && q[44] == 0) {
				int x1 = -2;
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " hoch " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == hoch(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + hoch(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[44] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
			if (frage == 45 && q[45] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level)-(Math.random() * (2 + 2 * level)));
				int x2 = 2 + (int) (Math.random() * 3);
				int x3 = 1+(int)(Math.random()*level);
				int a = readInt((int) hoch(x1, x2) + " hoch " + x3+"/" + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == hoch(x1,x3))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + hoch(x1,x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[45] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
			
			if (frage == 8 && q[8] == 0) {
				int x1 = 2;
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(3, level)) * x1;
				int a = readInt(x2 + " / " + x1 + "\n");
				if (a == x2 / x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x2 / x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[8] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 9 && q[9] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 4 * level));
				int x2 = 2;
				int a = readInt((int) Math.pow(x1, x2) + " ^ " + "1/" + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[9] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 10 && q[10] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 3 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				int a = readInt("Dezimal zu Binär(" + x1 + ")\n");
				if (Integer.toString(a).equals(Integer.toBinaryString(x1)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Integer.toBinaryString(x1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[10] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 11 && q[11] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 3 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				int a = readInt("Binär zu Dezimal(" + Integer.toBinaryString(x1) + ")\n");
				if (a == x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[11] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 12 && q[12] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				String a = readLine("Dezimal zu Hexadezimal(" + x1 + ")\n");
				if (a.equals(Integer.toHexString(x1)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Integer.toHexString(x1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[12] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 13 && q[13] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				int a = readInt("Hexadezimal zu Dezimal(" + Integer.toHexString(x1) + ")\n");
				if (a == x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[13] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 14 && q[14] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 10);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 5 * Math.pow(2, level)) * x1;
				int a = readInt(x2 + " / " + x1 + "\n");
				if (a == x2 / x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x2 / x1 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[14] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 15 && q[15] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 11);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 7 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " * " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 * x2)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x2 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[15] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 16 && q[16] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 7 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 11);
				int a = readInt(x1 + " * " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 * x2)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x2 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[16] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 17 && q[17] == 0) {
				double x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * (9 + 2 * level));
				double a = readDouble(x2 + " / " + (int) x1 + "\n");
				if (Math.round(a * 10000) == Math.round(x2 / x1 * 10000))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Math.round(x2 / x1 * 10000) / 10000.0 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[17] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 18 && q[18] == 0) {
				int x1 = -25 * level * level + (int) (Math.random() * level * 50 * level);
				int x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (8 + 2 * level));
				int a = readInt(x1 + " mod " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 % x2)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 % x2 + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[18] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 19 && q[19] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(2, level));
				int a = readInt("Ein Computersystem besitzt " + x1
						+ " virtuelle Seiten\nWie viele Bits werden für die Adressierung von diesen benötigt?");
				if (a == addBits(x1))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + addBits(x1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[19] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 20 && q[20] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) Math.pow(2, (int) (Math.random() * (level + 2)));
				int x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (level + 2));
				String a = readLine("Ein Computersystem besitzt " + x1 + " virtuelle Seiten und " + x2
						+ " Bit Seitenoffset(Byteadressierung)\nWie viel virtuellen Speicher hat das System?");
				if (einheit2Byte(a) == x1 * Math.pow(2, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * Math.pow(2, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[20] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 21 && q[21] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 10 * Math.pow(2, level));
				int a = readInt("Ein Computersystem besitzt " + x1
						+ " physische Seiten\nWie viele Bits werden für die Adressierung von diesen benötigt?");
				if (a == addBits(x1))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + addBits(x1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[21] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 22 && q[22] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) Math.pow(2, (int) (Math.random() * (level + 2)));
				int x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (level + 2));
				String a = readLine("Ein Computersystem besitzt " + x1 + " physische Seiten und " + x2
						+ " Bit Seitenoffset(Byteadressierung)\nWie viel physischen Speicher(Byte) hat das System?");
				if (einheit2Byte(a) == x1 * Math.pow(2, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * Math.pow(2, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[22] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 23 && q[23] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				int x3 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				int x4 = (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				String a = readLine(x2 + "/" + x1 + " + " + x4 + "/" + x3 + "\n");
				if (a.equals(bruchrechnenAdd(x2, x1, x4, x3)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + bruchrechnenAdd(x2, x1, x4, x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[23] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 24 && q[24] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				int x3 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				int x4 = (int) (Math.random() * 1.5 * level);
				String a = readLine(x2 + "/" + x1 + " - " + x4 + "/" + x3 + "\n");
				if (a.equals(bruchrechnenSub(x2, x1, x4, x3)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + bruchrechnenSub(x2, x1, x4, x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[24] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 25 && q[25] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x3 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x4 = (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				String a = readLine(x2 + "/" + x1 + " * " + x4 + "/" + x3 + "\n");
				if (a.equals(bruchrechnenMul(x2, x1, x4, x3)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + bruchrechnenMul(x2, x1, x4, x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[25] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 26 && q[26] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x2 = (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x3 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				int x4 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * 2 * level);
				String a = readLine(x2 + "/" + x1 + " : " + x4 + "/" + x3 + "\n");
				if (a.equals(bruchrechnenDiv(x2, x1, x4, x3)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + bruchrechnenDiv(x2, x1, x4, x3) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[26] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 27 && q[27] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (8 + 2 * level * level));
				int x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (8 + 2 * level * level));
				int a = readInt("größter gemeinsamer Teiler von " + x1 + " und " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == ggt(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + ggt(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[27] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 28 && q[28] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (8 + 2 * level));
				int x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (8 + 2 * level));
				int a = readInt("kleinstes gemeinsames Vielfaches von " + x1 + " und " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == x1 * x2 / ggt(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x2 / ggt(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[28] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 29 && q[29] == 0) {
				int[] reihe = zahlenreihen(level);
				int[] rh = new int[4];
				for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++)
					rh[i] = reihe[i];
				String s = Arrays.toString(rh);
				int a = readInt("nächste Zahl der Reihe: " + s + "\n");
				if (a == reihe[4])
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + reihe[4] + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[29] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 30 && q[30] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 0.5 * level));
				int x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 0.5 * level));
				int x3 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (2 + 0.5 * level));
				int x4 = (int) (Math.random() * (3 + 0.5 * level));
				String a = readLine("Welche Kapazität (K) hat eine Festplatte mit " + x1 + " Platten, " + x2
						+ " Zylindern, durchschnittlich " + x3 + " Sektoren pro Spurund " + x4 + " Byte pro Sektor?");
				if (einheit2ByteSI(a) == x1 * x2 * x3 * 2 * x4)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + x1 * x2 * x3 * 2 * x4 + " Byte ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[30] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 31 && q[31] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * (30 + 4 * level));
				String a = readLine("2 ^ " + x1 + " Byte\n");
				if (einheit2Byte(a) == Math.pow(2, x1))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + byte2Einheit(Math.pow(2, x1)) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[31] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 32 && q[32] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 3 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				String a = readLine("Binär zu Hexadezimal(" + Integer.toBinaryString(x1) + ")\n");
				if (a.equals(Integer.toHexString(x1)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Integer.toHexString(x1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[32] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 33 && q[33] == 0) {
				int x1 = (int) (Math.random() * 3 * Math.pow(1.5, level));
				String a = readLine("Hexadezimal zu Binär(" + Integer.toHexString(x1) + ")\n");
				if (a.contains("1"))
					a = a.substring(a.indexOf("1"));
				else
					a = "0";
				if (a.equals(Integer.toBinaryString(x1)))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Integer.toBinaryString(x1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[33] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 34 && q[34] == 0) {
				int x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (1 + 2 * level));
				int a = readInt("Bais einer Gleitkommazahl mit " + x1 + " Bit Exponent\n");
				if (a == Math.pow(2, x1 - 1) - 1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + (Math.pow(2, x1 - 1) - 1) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[34] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 35 && q[35] == 0) {
				int x1 = 2;
				int x2 = -1 - (int) (Math.random() * (2 + level));
				double a = readDouble(x1 + " ^ " + x2 + "\n");
				if (a == Math.pow(x1, x2))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + Math.pow(x1, x2) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[35] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 36 && q[36] == 0) {
				int x1, x2, x3, x4;
				x1 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (4 + level));
				x2 = 1 + (int) (Math.random() * (4 + level));
				x4 = (int) (Math.random() * (5 + level));
				if (Math.random() < 0.5)
					x3 = x1;
				else
					x3 = x2;
				int a = readInt(x1 + " * " + x2 + " + " + x3 + " * " + x4);
				if (a == x1 * x2 + x3 * x4)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + (x1 * x2 + x3 * x4) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[36] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 37 && q[37] == 0) {
				int x1 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);
				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);
				int x3 = (int) (Math.random() * (level + 1));
				double x4 = ((int) (Math.random() * 3)) / 2.0;
				double a = readInt("Elo A: " + x1 + "  Elo B: " + x2 + "  k: " + x3 + "  SA: " + x4);
				if (a == elo(x1, x2, x3, x4))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + elo(x1, x2, x3, x4) + " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[37] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 38 && q[38] == 0) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 5 *Math.pow(2, level));
				String loesung=longToNewLumini(x1);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine(x1 +" toLuminiString");
				if (a.equals(loesung))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + loesung+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[38] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 39 && q[39] == 0) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 5 *Math.pow(2, level));
				String input=longToNewLumini(x1);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				int  a = readInt(input +"toDecimal");
				if (a==x1)
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch!  " +x1+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[39] = -1;
				
				
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 40 && q[40] == 0) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3 *Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3 *Math.pow(2, level));
				String translate=longToNewLumini(x1);
				String translate2=longToNewLumini(x2);
				String loesung=longToNewLumini(x1+x2);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine(translate +"+"+ translate2);
				if (a.equals(loesung))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + loesung+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[40] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 41 && q[41] == 0) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3*Math.pow(2, level));
				int x2 =  (int) (Math.random() * 3 *Math.pow(2, level));
				String translate=longToNewLumini(x1);
				String translate2=longToNewLumini(x2);
			
				String loesung=longToNewLumini(x1-x2);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine(translate +"-"+ translate2);
				if (a.equals(loesung))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + loesung+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[41] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 42 && q[42] == 0) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 4* level);
				int x2 =  (int) (Math.random() * 4 *level);
				String translate=longToNewLumini(x1);
				String translate2=longToNewLumini(x2);
			
				String loesung=longToNewLumini(x1*x2);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine(translate +"x"+ translate2);
				if (a.equals(loesung))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " + loesung+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[43] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			if (frage == 43 && q[43] == 0) {
				int x1 =  (int) (Math.random() * 4* level);
				int x2 =  1+(int) (Math.random() * 4 *level);
				String translate=longToNewLumini(x1);
				String translate2=longToNewLumini(x2);
			
				String mullum=longToNewLumini(x1*x2);
//				int x2 = 500 + (int) (Math.random() * 2000);

				String a = readLine(mullum +"/"+ translate2);
				if (a.equals(translate))
					richtig++;
				else {
					println("Falsch! " +translate+ " ist richtig");
					break;
				}
				q[43] = -1;
				counter++;
			}
			
		}
		

		if (richtig < level * 10) {
			bonuszeit = 0;
			consecutiveErrors++;
			String s = null;
			if (richtig <= 7)
				s = "Du musst noch viel lernen!";
			if (richtig > 7)
				s = "Sehr löblich!";
			if (richtig >= 15)
				s = "Nice!";
			if (richtig >= 30)
				s = "Respekt!";
			if (richtig >= 50)
				{consecutiveErrors=0;
				s = "Unerreichbar!";}
			if (richtig >= 75)
				s = "Godlike!";
			if (richtig >= 100)
				s = "Unbesiegbar!";
			print(richtig + " Punkte" + "\n" + s + "\n");
			highscore(richtig);
			
			// NEU: Der Circuit Breaker löst aus!
            if (consecutiveErrors >= 3) {
                println("3 Fehlversuche ohne mindestens 50 Punkte. Das System-Rauschen ist zu hoch.");
                println("Der 'Härter Foltern'-Schutzschalter ist aktiviert.");
                println("Bitte 15 Sekunden tief durchatmen. Soziale Integrität wird geladen...");
                println("Bitte kurz in KI-Game mit Sprachmodell analysieren. Vielen Dank, Let's Go");
                
                try {
                    // Zwingt den Thread (und deinen Geist) für 15 Sekunden zur Ruhe
                    Thread.sleep(15000); 
                } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                    // Ignorieren
                }
                
                println("Du kannst jetzt entspannt weiter machen!\n");
                
                // Reset des Fehlversuchzählers nach der erfolgreichen Pause
                consecutiveErrors = 0; 
            }
			
			int neu = 0;
			while (neu != 1) {
				neu = readInt("1 = Erneut spielen, 2 = Highscore, 3 = Ende\n");
				if (neu == 2)
					showHighscore();
				if (neu == 3)
					sicher = readInt("Wirklich beenden?\n1 = Ja, 2 = Nein\n");
				if (sicher == 1)
					exit();
				if (neu == 1) {
					level = 1;
					richtig = 0;
					start = 0;
					run();
				}
			}
		} else {
			bonuszeit = zeitbegrenzung - zeit;
			level++;
			run();
		}
	}

	public void highscore(double punkte) {
		int i = 0;
		if (score[0][0] == null)
			for (i = 0; i <= 9; i++) {
				score[i][0] = "0";
				score[i][1] = "";
			}
		for (i = 0; i <= 9; i++) {
			if (richtig > Double.valueOf(score[i][0])) {
				Double scoreDouble = new Double(richtig);
				String s = scoreDouble.toString();
				for (int j = 9; j >= 1; j--) {
					score[i + j][0] = score[i + j - 1][0];
					score[i + j][1] = score[i + j - 1][1];
				}
				score[i][0] = s;
				score[i][1] = readLine("Name:");
				break;
			}
		}

	}

	public void showHighscore() {
		println(score[0][0] + " " + score[0][1] + "\n" + score[1][0] + " " + score[1][1] + "\n" + score[2][0] + " "
				+ score[2][1] + "\n" + score[3][0] + " " + score[3][1] + "\n" + score[4][0] + " " + score[4][1] + "\n"
				+ score[5][0] + " " + score[5][1] + "\n" + score[6][0] + " " + score[6][1] + "\n" + score[7][0] + " "
				+ score[7][1] + "\n" + score[8][0] + " " + score[8][1] + "\n" + score[9][0] + " " + score[9][1] + "\n");
	}

	public int addBits(int i) {
		if (i == 1)
			return 1;
		double d = Math.log(i) / Math.log(2);
		int a = (d == (int) d) ? (int) d : ((int) d) + 1;
		return a;
	}

	public int ggt(int n1, int n2) {
		n1 = Math.abs(n1);
		n2 = Math.abs(n2);
		while (n2 != 0) {
			if (n1 > n2)
				n1 -= n2;
			else
				n2 -= n1;
		}
		return n1;
	}

	public String bruchrechnen(int ze, int ne) {
		int zahl = 0;
		int teiler = ggt(ne, ze);
		ze /= teiler;
		ne /= teiler;
		if (ne == 0)
			return "0";
		if (ne == 1)
			return String.valueOf(ze);
		zahl = ze / ne;
		if (zahl != 0)
			return (zahl + " " + ze % ne + "/" + ne);
		return (ze + "/" + ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenAdd(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * n2 + z2 * n1;
		int ne = n1 * n2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenSub(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * n2 - z2 * n1;
		int ne = n1 * n2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenMul(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * z2;
		int ne = n1 * n2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public String bruchrechnenDiv(int z1, int n1, int z2, int n2) {
		int ze = z1 * n2;
		int ne = n1 * z2;
		return bruchrechnen(ze, ne);
	}

	public int[] zahlenreihen(int level) {
		int[] reihe1 = new int[5];
		int[] reihe2 = new int[4];
		int[] reihe3 = new int[3];
		int[] reihe4 = new int[2];
		reihe1[0] = (int) (Math.random() * (level + 3));
		reihe2[0] = (int) (Math.random() * (level + 3));
		reihe3[0] = (int) Math.max((Math.random() * level - 0.8), 0);
		reihe4[0] = (int) Math.max((Math.random() * level - 2.5), 0);
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe1[0] *= -1;
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe2[0] *= -1;
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe3[0] *= -1;
		if (Math.random() < Math.min(0.5, level * 0.1))
			reihe4[0] *= -1;
		for (int i = 1; i < 2; i++) {
			reihe4[i] = reihe4[i - 1];
		}
		for (int i = 1; i < 3; i++) {
			reihe3[i] = reihe3[i - 1] + reihe4[i - 1];
		}
		for (int i = 1; i < 4; i++) {
			reihe2[i] = reihe2[i - 1] + reihe3[i - 1];
		}
		for (int i = 1; i < 5; i++) {
			reihe1[i] = reihe1[i - 1] + reihe2[i - 1];
		}
		return reihe1;
	}

	double einheit2Byte(String s) {
		s = s.toLowerCase();
		double z;
		if (s.contains("ebyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("ebyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 6);
		} else if (s.contains("p")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("p")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 5);
		} else if (s.contains("tbyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("tbyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 4);
		} else if (s.contains("g")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("g")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 3);
		} else if (s.contains("m")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("m")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 2);
		} else if (s.contains("k")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("k")));
			return z * Math.pow(1024, 1);
		} else if (s.contains("byte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("byte")));
			return z;
		} else
			return Double.valueOf(s);
	}

	double einheit2ByteSI(String s) {
		s = s.toLowerCase();
		double z;
		if (s.contains("ebyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("ebyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 6);
		} else if (s.contains("p")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("p")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 5);
		} else if (s.contains("tbyte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("tbyte")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 4);
		} else if (s.contains("g")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("g")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 3);
		} else if (s.contains("m")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("m")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 2);
		} else if (s.contains("k")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("k")));
			return z * Math.pow(1000, 1);
		} else if (s.contains("byte")) {
			z = Double.valueOf(s.substring(0, s.indexOf("byte")));
			return z;
		} else
			return Double.valueOf(s);
	}

	String byte2Einheit(double d) {
		String e = "";
		String z = "";
		if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 6)) {
			e = " EByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 6));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 5)) {
			e = " PByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 5));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 4)) {
			e = " TByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 4));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 5)) {
			e = " GByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 3));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 2)) {
			e = " MByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 2));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1024, 1)) {
			e = " KByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1024, 1));
		} else {
			e = " Byte";
			z = String.valueOf(d);
		}
		return z + e;
	}

	String byte2EinheitSI(double d) {
		String e = "";
		String z = "";
		if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 6)) {
			e = " EByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 6));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 5)) {
			e = " PByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 5));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 4)) {
			e = " TByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 4));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 5)) {
			e = " GByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 3));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 2)) {
			e = " MByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 2));
		} else if (d >= Math.pow(1000, 1)) {
			e = " KByte";
			z = String.valueOf(d / Math.pow(1000, 1));
		} else {
			e = " Byte";
			z = String.valueOf(d);
		}
		return z + e;
	}

	public int[] nextSqrt(int i) {
		int[] t = { 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0 };
		int max = 0;
		int[] ret = { 0, 0 };
		while (Math.pow(t[0], 2) <= i) {
			t[0]++;
		}
		t[0]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[0], 2)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[0], 2);
			ret[0] = t[0];
			ret[1] = 2;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[1], 3) <= i) {
			t[1]++;
		}
		t[1]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[1], 3)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[1], 3);
			ret[0] = t[1];
			ret[1] = 3;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[2], 4) <= i) {
			t[2]++;
		}
		t[2]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[2], 4)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[2], 4);
			ret[0] = t[2];
			ret[1] = 4;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[3], 5) <= i) {
			t[3]++;
		}
		t[3]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[3], 5)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[3], 5);
			ret[0] = t[3];
			ret[1] = 5;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[4], 6) <= i) {
			t[4]++;
		}
		t[4]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[4], 6)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[4], 6);
			ret[0] = t[4];
			ret[1] = 6;
		}
		while (Math.pow(t[5], 7) <= i) {
			t[5]++;
		}
		t[5]--;
		if (max < Math.pow(t[5], 7)) {
			max = (int) Math.pow(t[5], 7);
			ret[0] = t[5];
			ret[1] = 7;
		}

		return ret;

	}

	public int elo(int RA, int RB, int k, double SA) {
		double EA = 1 / (1 + Math.pow(10, (RB - RA) / 400.0));
		double RAnew = RA + k * (SA - EA);
		if (RAnew >= 0)
			RAnew += 0.5;
		else
			RAnew -= 0.5;
		return (int) RAnew;
	}
	
	
	public static long newLuminiNumberToDecimal(String newLuminiNumber, int basis) {
		int lenge = newLuminiNumber.length();
		long number = getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers2(lenge - 1, basis);;

		number+=basisNStringToLong(newLuminiNumber,basis);
		return number;
	}
	public static long getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers2(int LumNeuLänge, int LumNeuBasis) {
		if(LumNeuLänge==0)return 0;
		long output = 0;
		for (int i = 1; i <= LumNeuLänge; i++) {
			output += (Math.pow(LumNeuBasis, i));
		}

		return output;
	}
	
	public static long basisNStringToLong(String basNStr, int basis) {
		int lenge = basNStr.length();
		long output = 0;
		int symbol = 0;
		for (int i = lenge - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '0')
				symbol = 0;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '1')
				symbol = 1;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '2')
				symbol = 2;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '3')
				symbol = 3;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '4')
				symbol = 4;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '5')
				symbol = 5;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '6')
				symbol = 6;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '7')
				symbol = 7;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '8')
				symbol = 8;
			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '9')
				symbol = 9;
			
			output+=(symbol*Math.pow(basis, (lenge - 1-i)));
		}
		return output;
	}
	
	
	public double x(double faktor1, double faktor2) {
		double produkt=faktor1*faktor2;
		produkt=Math.abs(produkt);
		if(faktor1<0||faktor2<0)produkt=-produkt;		
		return produkt;		
	}
	
	public double hoch(double basis, double exponent){
		boolean negativ=false;
		if(basis<0)negativ=true;
		basis=Math.abs(basis);
		double result=Math.pow(basis, exponent);
		if(negativ)result=-result;
		return result;
	}
	
	
	public String longToNewLumini(long input) {
	    // Sicherheitsprüfung für negative Eingaben
	    if (input < 0) {
	        return "-"+  longToNewLumini(-input) ;
	    }

	    // Die gewünschte Sequenz ist:
	    // Index 0-1: Länge 1 (Anzahl: 2^1 = 2) -> "0", "1"
	    // Index 2-5: Länge 2 (Anzahl: 2^2 = 4) -> "00", "01", "10", "11"
	    // Index 6-13: Länge 3 (Anzahl: 2^3 = 8) -> "000", ...

	    long currentLength = 1; // Wir beginnen mit der Länge 1
	    long bucketSize = 2;   // Die Anzahl der Werte für die aktuelle Länge (2^currentLength)

	    // Wir iterieren durch die Längen-Klassen.
	    // Solange unser 'input' (der Index) größer oder gleich der Anzahl der Werte
	    // in der aktuellen Klasse ist, ziehen wir diese Anzahl ab und gehen zur nächsten Länge.
	    while (input >= bucketSize) {
	        input -= bucketSize; // Ziehe die Größe der aktuellen Klasse ab
	        currentLength++;     // Erhöhe die Länge für die nächste Klasse
	        bucketSize *= 2;    // Verdopple die Größe für die nächste Klasse (2^(newLength))
	    }

	    // Wenn die Schleife endet, ist 'input' der korrekte, 0-basierte Offset
	    // innerhalb der Klasse mit der Länge 'currentLength'.

	    // Wandle diesen Offset in einen Binär-String um.
	    String output = Long.toBinaryString(input);

	    // Füge führende Nullen hinzu, damit der String die korrekte Länge (currentLength) erreicht.
	    while (output.length() < currentLength) {
	        output = "0" + output;
	    }

	    return output;
	}
	
	

	public static void main(String[] args) {
		new MatheFuerInformatiker().start(args);
	}
}

			+ "	public static void makeLuminiStrings(boolean invertString) {\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < LuminiStrings.length; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			String basisNumber = intToBasisNString(i,basis,false);\r\n"
			+ "			if(newLumini)basisNumber=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i,basis);\r\n"
			+ "			if (invertString)\r\n"
			+ "				basisNumber = invertString(basisNumber);\r\n"
			+ "			\r\n"
			+ "			char[] luminiSyms= luminiSymbols;\r\n"
			+ "			String LuminiString = changeNumberToLuminiSymbols(basisNumber,luminiSyms);\r\n"
			+ "			\r\n"
			+ "//			if(binaryLumini)LuminiString=morseToBinaryLumini(LuminiString);\r\n"
			+ "			\r\n"
			+ "			\r\n"
			+ "			LuminiStrings[i] = LuminiString;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static void initLumLetters(String addBits, String zeichensatz) {\r\n"
			+ "		for(int i=0; i<zeichensatz.length()&&i<256; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "		LetterToLumini.put(zeichensatz.charAt(i), addBits+LuminiStrings[i]);\r\n"
			+ "	}}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String invertString(String string) {\r\n"
			+ "		String invertString = \"\";\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < string.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			invertString = string.charAt(i) + invertString;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		return invertString;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"

			+ "	// Text zu Lumini\r\n"
			+ "	public static String toLumini(String text) {\r\n"
			+ "		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();\r\n"
			+ "		for (char c : text.toCharArray()) {\r\n"
			+ "			if (LetterToLumini.containsKey(c)) {\r\n"
			+ "				sb.append(LetterToLumini.get(c)).append(spaceSym);\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		String output =  sb.toString();\r\n"
			+ "		output=output.trim();\r\n"
			+ "		if(binaryLumini&&translatetyp==1)output=morseToBinary(output);\r\n"
			+ "		if(binaryLumini&&translatetyp==2)output=morseToBinaryLumini2(output);\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "// Lumini -> Klartext\r\n"
			+ "	public static String fromLumini(String morse) {\r\n"
			+ "		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();\r\n"
			+ "		String[] LuminiCodes = morse.split(spaceSym);\r\n"
			+ "		for (String LuminiCode : LuminiCodes) {\r\n"
			+ "			if (LuminiToLetter.containsKey(LuminiCode)) {\r\n"
			+ "				sb.append(LuminiToLetter.get(LuminiCode));\r\n"
			+ "			} else if (LuminiCode.equals(spaceSym)) {\r\n"
			+ "				sb.append(\" \");\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return sb.toString();\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"

			+ "			    // zeichenfolge2 = zeichenfolge1;\r\n"
			+ "			    // zeichenfolge3 = zeichenfolge1;\r\n"

			+ "			// ...\r\n"
			+ "			case 11:\r\n"
			+ "			    System.out.print(\"spaceSym1 (Trenner zwischen Lumini-Codes): \");\r\n"
			+ "			    spaceSym=scanner.next();\r\n"
			+ "			    System.out.print(\"spaceSym2 (Lumini-Code für Leerzeichen): \");\r\n"
			+ "			    spaceSym2=scanner.next();\r\n"
			+ "			    reinitializeLuminiMappings(); // ❗ Füge diesen Aufruf hinzu\r\n"
			+ "			    break;\r\n"
			+ "			case 12:\r\n"
			+ "			    binaryLumini=scanner.nextBoolean();\r\n"
			+ "			    reinitializeLuminiMappings(); // ❗ Füge diesen Aufruf hinzu\r\n"
			+ "			    break;\r\n"
			+ "			case 13:\r\n"
			+ "				System.out.println(\"Choose number of translationTasks per round\");\r\n"
			+ "			    translationQuests=scanner.nextInt();\r\n"
			+ "			    break;\r\n"
			+ "			case 14:\r\n"
			+ "				System.out.println(\"Enter String to translate in Lumini: \");\r\n"
			+ "				\r\n"
			+ "			    String input=translateString;\r\n"
			+ "			    String output=toLumini(input);\r\n"
			+ "			    System.out.println(output);\r\n"
			+ "			    break;\r\n"
			+ "			case 0:\r\n"
			+ "				running = false;\r\n"
			+ "				System.out.println(\"Spiel beendet. Endstand: \" + motivationPoints + \" Punkte.\");\r\n"
			+ "				break;\r\n"
			+ "			default:\r\n"
			+ "				System.out.println(\"Ungültige Auswahl!\\n\");\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		scanner.close();\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"

			+ "	// Transformationen\r\n"
			+ "	public static String doubleToBasisN(double value, int basis, int nachkommastellen, char kommazeichen,\r\n"
			+ "			boolean basisangabe) {\r\n"
			+ "		double nachkommaanteil = value - (int) (value);\r\n"
			+ "		String nachkommaanteilStr = NachkommaanteilToBasisNString(nachkommaanteil, basis, nachkommastellen);\r\n"
			+ "		String vorkommaanteil = intToBasisNString((int) (value), basis, false);\r\n"
			+ "		String output = vorkommaanteil;\r\n"
			+ "		output = output + kommazeichen + nachkommaanteilStr;\r\n"
			+ "		if (basisangabe)\r\n"
			+ "			output = output + \"(Basis:\" + basis + \")\";\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String NachkommaanteilToBasisNString(double value, int basis, int tiefe) {\r\n"
			+ "		StringBuilder nachkommaanteil = new StringBuilder();\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < tiefe; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			// Multipliziere den Wert mit der Basis\r\n"
			+ "			value *= basis;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "			// Extrahiere den ganzzahligen Teil (die neue Ziffer in der Zielbasis)\r\n"
			+ "			int ziffer = (int) value;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "			// Füge die Ziffer an den String an\r\n"
			+ "			nachkommaanteil.append(ziffer);\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "			// Subtrahiere den extrahierten Teil, um den neuen Nachkommaanteil zu erhalten\r\n"
			+ "			value -= ziffer;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "			// Beende die Schleife, wenn der Nachkommaanteil null ist\r\n"
			+ "			if (value == 0) {\r\n"
			+ "				break;\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return nachkommaanteil.toString();\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String changeNumberToLuminiSymbols(String basisNString, char[] luminiSymbols) {\r\n"
			+ "	    String output = basisNString;\r\n"
			+ "	    for (int i = 0; i < luminiSymbols.length; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "	        String numberString = String.valueOf(i); // <-- Hier ist die Änderung\r\n"
			+ "	        char luminiSymbol = luminiSymbols[i];\r\n"
			+ "	        output = output.replace(numberString, String.valueOf(luminiSymbol));\r\n"
			+ "	    }\r\n"
			+ "	    return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public String longTonewLumini(long input) {\r\n"
			+ "		double div= Math.exp(2);\r\n"
			+ "		double size= Math.exp(input);\r\n"
			+ "		size=size/div;\r\n"
			+ "		String output=\"\";\r\n"
			+ "		for(int i=0;i<size; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			output=output+\".\";\r\n"
			+ "			\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String intToBasisNString(int value, int basis, boolean basisanzeige) {\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		String output2 = \"0\";\r\n"
			+ "		if (basisanzeige)\r\n"
			+ "			output2 = output2 + \"(Basis:\" + basis + \")\";\r\n"
			+ "		if (value == 0)\r\n"
			+ "			return output2;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		boolean negativ = false;\r\n"
			+ "		if (value < 0)\r\n"
			+ "			negativ = true;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(); // Vorteile der Klasse Stringbuilder erforschen\r\n"
			+ "		while (value != 0) {\r\n"
			+ "			int modulo = value % basis;\r\n"
			+ "			sb.append(modulo);\r\n"
			+ "			value = value - modulo;\r\n"
			+ "			value /= basis;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		String output = sb.toString();\r\n"
			+ "		output = inverString(output);\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		output = output.replace(\"-\", \"\");\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		if (negativ)\r\n"
			+ "			output = \"-\" + output;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		if (basisanzeige)\r\n"
			+ "			output = output + \"(Basis:\" + basis + \")\";\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	// reinitialisierung\r\n"
			+ "	public static void reinitializeLuminiMappings() {\r\n"
			+ "	    // 1. Mappings leeren, um alte Werte zu entfernen\r\n"
			+ "	    LetterToLumini.clear();\r\n"
			+ "	    LuminiToLetter.clear();\r\n"
			+ "	    \r\n"
			+ "	    // 2. Lumini-Strings neu generieren (abhängig von basis, newLumini, invertNumber)\r\n"
			+ "	    makeLuminiStrings(invertNumber);\r\n"
			+ "	    \r\n"
			+ "	    // 3. Neue Zeichensatz-Steuerung\r\n"
			+ "	    initLumLetters(\"\",zeichenfolge1);\r\n"
			+ "	    initLumLetters(\"\",zeichenfolge2);\r\n"
			+ "	    initLumLetters(\"\",zeichenfolge3);\r\n"
			+ "	    \r\n"
			+ "	    // 4. Leerzeichen\r\n"
			+ "	    LetterToLumini.put(' ', spaceSym2);\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	    // 5. Umkehrabbildung neu erstellen\r\n"
			+ "	    for (Map.Entry<Character, String> entry : LetterToLumini.entrySet()) {\r\n"
			+ "	        LuminiToLetter.put(entry.getValue(), entry.getKey());\r\n"
			+ "	    }\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String inverString(String string) {\r\n"
			+ "		StringBuilder output = new StringBuilder();\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = string.length() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\r\n"
			+ "			output.append(string.charAt(i));\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return output.toString();\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "//	\r\n"
			+ "//	Public String intToLuminString(int value) {\r\n"
			+ "//		Integer\r\n"
			+ "//	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static int LuminiStringToInt(String LuminiString) {\r\n"
			+ "		int summer = 1;\r\n"
			+ "		int value = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = LuminiString.length() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\r\n"
			+ "			if (LuminiString.charAt(i) == '-') {\r\n"
			+ "				value += summer;\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "			summer *= 2;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return value;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static int charToInt(char c) {\r\n"
			+ "		return (int) c;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static char intToChar(int i) {\r\n"
			+ "		return (char) i;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static char[] string2(String string) {\r\n"
			+ "		char[] newString = new char[string.length()];\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < string.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			newString[i] = string.charAt(i);\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return newString;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String doubleToHexSting(double wert) {\r\n"
			+ "		String hexString = Double.toHexString(wert); // Beginnt mit (0x)=(Basis16); endet mit py=*2^y\r\n"
			+ "		return hexString;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String doubleToHexStingLumini(double wert) {\r\n"
			+ "		String hexString = Double.toHexString(wert); // Beginnt mit (0x)=(Basis16); endet mit py=*2^y\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString.replace(\"0x\", \"\");\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString + \"(Basis=16)\";\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString.replace(\"p\", \"*2^\");\r\n"
			+ "		return hexString;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String doubleToBinStingLumini(double wert) {\r\n"
			+ "		String hexString = Double.toHexString(wert); // Beginnt mit (0x)=(Basis16); endet mit py=*2^y\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString.replace(\"0x\", \"\");\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString + \"\";\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString.replace(\"p\", \"*2^\");\r\n"
			+ "		String binString = hexString.replace(\"0\", \"0000\").replace(\"1\", \"0001\").replace(\"2\", \"0010\").replace(\"3\", \"0011\")\r\n"
			+ "				.replace(\"4\", \"0100\");\r\n"
			+ "		binString = binString.replace(\"5\", \"0101\").replace(\"6\", \"0110\").replace(\"7\", \"0111\").replace(\"8\", \"1000\")\r\n"
			+ "				.replace(\"9\", \"1001\").replace(\"a\", \"1010\").replace(\"b\", \"1011\").replace(\"c\", \"1100\")\r\n"
			+ "				.replace(\"d\", \"1101\").replace(\"e\", \"1110\").replace(\"f\", \"1111\");\r\n"
			+ "		return binString;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String doubleToLuminiSting(double wert) {\r\n"
			+ "		String hexString = Double.toHexString(wert); // Beginnt mit (0x)=(Basis16); endet mit py=*2^y\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString.replace(\"0x\", \"\");\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString + \"\";\r\n"
			+ "		hexString = hexString.replace(\"p\", \"*2^\");\r\n"
			+ "		String binString = hexString.replace(\"0\", \"0000\").replace(\"1\", \"0001\").replace(\"2\", \"0010\").replace(\"3\", \"0011\")\r\n"
			+ "				.replace(\"4\", \"0100\");\r\n"
			+ "		binString = binString.replace(\"5\", \"0101\").replace(\"6\", \"0110\").replace(\"7\", \"0111\").replace(\"8\", \"1000\")\r\n"
			+ "				.replace(\"9\", \"1001\").replace(\"a\", \"1010\").replace(\"b\", \"1011\").replace(\"c\", \"1100\")\r\n"
			+ "				.replace(\"d\", \"1101\").replace(\"e\", \"1110\").replace(\"f\", \"1111\");\r\n"
			+ "		binString = binString.replace(\".\", \",\");\r\n"
			+ "		binString = binString.replace(\"1\", \"-\").replace(\"0\", \".\");\r\n"
			+ "		return binString;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	// Fehlerhaft\r\n"
			+ "	public static double LuminiToDouble(String luminiString) {\r\n"
			+ "		int[] bits = new int[luminiString.length()];\r\n"
			+ "		int vorkommastellen = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		int exponent = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		int expAdd = 1;\r\n"
			+ "		boolean afterExp = false;\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < luminiString.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "			if (luminiString.charAt(i) == '*')\r\n"
			+ "				break;\r\n"
			+ "			if (luminiString.charAt(i) == ',') {\r\n"
			+ "				vorkommastellen = i;\r\n"
			+ "				continue;\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "			if (luminiString.charAt(i) == '-')\r\n"
			+ "				if (afterExp == false)\r\n"
			+ "					bits[i] = 1;\r\n"
			+ "				else {\r\n"
			+ "					exponent += expAdd;\r\n"
			+ "					expAdd *= 2;\r\n"
			+ "				}\r\n"
			+ "			if (afterExp)\r\n"
			+ "				expAdd *= 2;\r\n"
			+ "			if (luminiString.charAt(i) == '^')\r\n"
			+ "				afterExp = true;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		double wert = 0;\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		double adder = Math.pow(2, vorkommastellen + exponent);\r\n"
			+ "		for (int j = 0; j < bits.length; j++) {\r\n"
			+ "			if (bits[j] == 1)\r\n"
			+ "				wert += adder;\r\n"
			+ "			adder /= 2;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return wert;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static long getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers(int LumNeuLänge, int LumNeuBasis) {\r\n"
			+ "		if(LumNeuLänge==0)return 0;\r\n"
			+ "		long output = -1;\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 1; i <= LumNeuLänge; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			output += (Math.pow(LumNeuBasis, i));\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static long getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers2(int LumNeuLänge, int LumNeuBasis) {\r\n"
			+ "		if(LumNeuLänge==0)return 0;\r\n"
			+ "		long output = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 1; i <= LumNeuLänge; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			output += (Math.pow(LumNeuBasis, i));\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static long basisNStringToLong(String basNStr, int basis) {\r\n"
			+ "		int lenge = basNStr.length();\r\n"
			+ "		long output = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		int symbol = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = lenge - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '0')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 0;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '1')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 1;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '2')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 2;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '3')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 3;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '4')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 4;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '5')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 5;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '6')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 6;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '7')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 7;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '8')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 8;\r\n"
			+ "			if (basNStr.charAt(i) == '9')\r\n"
			+ "				symbol = 9;\r\n"
			+ "			\r\n"
			+ "			output+=(symbol*Math.pow(basis, (lenge - 1-i)));\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public double newLuminiToDouble(String newLuminiNumber) {\r\n"
			+ "		double basis = 2;\r\n"
			+ "		int size =newLuminiNumber.length();\r\n"
			+ "		double pow=Math.pow(basis, size);\r\n"
			+ "		double zero=pow-2;\r\n"
			+ "		double einheit=1;\r\n"
			+ "double output=zero;\r\n"
			+ "		for(int i=0; i<size; i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			if(newLuminiNumber.indexOf(i)==1)output+=einheit;\r\n"
			+ "			einheit+=basis;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "//public String newLuminiString(long l) {\r\n"
			+ "//	String output=\"j\";\r\n"
			+ "//	return output;\r\n"
			+ "//}\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static long newLuminiNumberToDecimal(String newLuminiNumber, int basis) {\r\n"
			+ "		int lenge = newLuminiNumber.length();\r\n"
			+ "		long number = getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers(lenge - 1, basis)+1;\r\n"
			+ "		if(lenge==1)number=0;\r\n"
			+ "		number+=basisNStringToLong(newLuminiNumber,basis);\r\n"
			+ "		return number;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static int highestLum(long decimal, int basis) {\r\n"
			+ "		int count=0;\r\n"
			+ "		while (getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers(count,basis)<decimal) {\r\n"
			+ "			count++;	\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return count;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static String decimalToNewLuminiNumber(long decimal, int basis) {\r\n"
			+ "		String newLuminiNumber=\"\";\r\n"
			+ "		int length=highestLum(decimal,basis);\r\n"
			+ "		long cutdecimal=decimal-getLuminiBasisNeuNumbers2(length-1,basis);\r\n"
			+ "		newLuminiNumber=intToBasisNString((int) cutdecimal,basis,false);\r\n"
			+ "		while(newLuminiNumber.length()<length)newLuminiNumber=\"0\"+newLuminiNumber;\r\n"
			+ "		return newLuminiNumber;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static String makeSameSyms(String symElem, int anzahl) {\r\n"
			+ "		String output=\"\";\r\n"
			+ "		for(int i=0; i<anzahl;i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			output=output+symElem;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return output;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	// Eigene Übersetzung: Geeignet für Schrift, für Audio oder Visuel\r\n"
			+ "	// möglicherweise etwas schwer korrekt zu verstehen\r\n"
			+ "	public static String morseToBinaryLumini(String morse) {\r\n"
			+ "		String binary = \"\";\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < morse.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			char current = morse.charAt(i);\r\n"
			+ "			if (current == '.')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"-\";\r\n"
			+ "			else if (current == '-')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"--\";\r\n"
			+ "			else if (current == ' ')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"\";\r\n"
			+ "//			else if (current == '/')\r\n"
			+ "//				binary = binary + \"|\";\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "			if(i<morse.length()-1 )binary= binary + \"|\";\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return binary;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static String morseToBinaryLumini2(String morse) {\r\n"
			+ "		String binary = \"\";\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < morse.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			char current = morse.charAt(i);\r\n"
			+ "			if (current == '.')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"|\";\r\n"
			+ "			else if (current == '-')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"-\";\r\n"
			+ "			else if (current == ' ')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"--\";\r\n"
			+ "			else if (current == '/')\r\n"
			+ "				binary = binary + \"---\";\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return binary;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "	\r\n"
			+ "	public static String binaryLuminiToMorse2(String binLumini) {\r\n"
			+ "		binLumini = binLumini.replace(\"||\",\"/\");\r\n"
			+ "		binLumini = binLumini.replace(\"\",\" \");\r\n"
			+ "		binLumini = binLumini.replace(\"-\",\"-\");\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "		return binLumini;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "	public static String binaryLuminiToMorse(String binaryLumini) {\r\n"
			+ "		String morse = \"\";\r\n"
			+ "		int strichcount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		int trenncount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "		for (int i = 0; i < binaryLumini.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "			char current = binaryLumini.charAt(i);\r\n"
			+ "			if (current == '-') {\r\n"
			+ "				strichcount++;\r\n"
			+ "				trenncount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "			} else if (current == '|') {\r\n"
			+ "				trenncount++;\r\n"
			+ "				if (strichcount == 0)\r\n"
			+ "					if (trenncount == 2)\r\n"
			+ "						morse = morse + \" \";\r\n"
			+ "				if (trenncount == 3)\r\n"
			+ "					morse = morse + \"/\";\r\n"
			+ "				if (strichcount == 1)\r\n"
			+ "					morse = morse + \".\";\r\n"
			+ "				if (strichcount == 2)\r\n"
			+ "					morse = morse + \"-\";\r\n"
			+ "				strichcount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		return morse;\r\n"
			+ "	}\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "		public static String morseToBinary(String morse) {\r\n"
			+ "			String binary = \"\";\r\n"
			+ "			for (int i = 0; i < morse.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "				char current = morse.charAt(i);\r\n"
			+ "				if (current == '.')\r\n"
			+ "					binary = binary + makeSameSyms(\"-\",dotLength);\r\n"
			+ "				else if (current == '-')\r\n"
			+ "					binary = binary + makeSameSyms(\"-\",dashLength);\r\n"
			+ "				else if (current == ' ')\r\n"
			+ "					binary = binary + makeSameSyms(\"|\",spaceBetweenLetters-2*spacBetweenPartsOfSameLetter);\r\n"
			+ "				else if (current == '/')\r\n"
			+ "					binary = binary + makeSameSyms(\"|\",spaceBetweenWords-2*(spaceBetweenLetters-2*spacBetweenPartsOfSameLetter)-4*spacBetweenPartsOfSameLetter);\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "				\r\n"
			+ "				if(i!=morse.length()-1&&current != '/') binary=binary + makeSameSyms(\"|\",spacBetweenPartsOfSameLetter);\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "			return binary;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "		\r\n"
			+ "\r\n"
			+ "		public static String binaryToMorse(String binaryLumini) {\r\n"
			+ "			String morse = \"\";\r\n"
			+ "			int strichcount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "			int trenncount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "			for (int i = 0; i < binaryLumini.length(); i++) {\r\n"
			+ "				char current = binaryLumini.charAt(i);\r\n"
			+ "				if (current == '-') {\r\n"
			+ "					strichcount++;\r\n"
			+ "					trenncount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "				} else if (current == '|') {\r\n"
			+ "					trenncount++;\r\n"
			+ "					if (strichcount == 0)\r\n"
			+ "						if (trenncount == spacBetweenPartsOfSameLetter)\r\n"
			+ "							morse = morse + \" \";\r\n"
			+ "					if (trenncount == spaceBetweenLetters)\r\n"
			+ "						morse = morse + \"/\";\r\n"
			+ "					if (strichcount == dotLength)\r\n"
			+ "						morse = morse + \".\";\r\n"
			+ "					if (strichcount == dashLength)\r\n"
			+ "						morse = morse + \"-\";\r\n"
			+ "					strichcount = 0;\r\n"
			+ "				}\r\n"
			+ "			}\r\n"
			+ "			return morse;\r\n"
			+ "		}\r\n"

			+ "//\r\n"

	static String[] generateWords() {
		String words[]=new String[1000];
		for(int i=0; i<1000;i++) {
			String string1=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i,basis);
			String string2=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i+1,basis);
			String string3=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i+2,basis);
			String string4=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i+3,basis);
			String string5=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i+4,basis);
			for(int j=zeichensatz.length()-1; j>=0;j--) {
			string1=string1.replace(decimalToNewLuminiNumber(j,basis), (zeichensatz.charAt(j)+"")).trim();
			string2=string2.replace(decimalToNewLuminiNumber(j,basis), (zeichensatz.charAt(j)+"")).trim();
			string3=string3.replace(decimalToNewLuminiNumber(j,basis), (zeichensatz.charAt(j)+"")).trim();
			string4=string1.replace(decimalToNewLuminiNumber(j,basis), (zeichensatz.charAt(j)+"")).trim();
			string5=string2.replace(decimalToNewLuminiNumber(j,basis), (zeichensatz.charAt(j)+"")).trim();
			
			
			}
			string1=string1+string2+string3+string4+string5;
			words[i]=string1;
		}
		return words;
	}

	public static void fillTrainingWordList(double level) {
		words2.clear();
		for(int i=0; i<level; i++) {
			words2.add(words[i]);
		}
	}

	public static void makeLuminiStrings(boolean invertString) {
		for (int i = 0; i < LuminiStrings.length; i++) {
			String basisNumber = intToBasisNString(i,basis,false);
			if(newLumini)basisNumber=decimalToNewLuminiNumber(i,basis);
			if (invertString)
				basisNumber = invertString(basisNumber);
			
			char[] luminiSyms= luminiSymbols;
			String LuminiString = changeNumberToLuminiSymbols(basisNumber,luminiSyms);
			
//			if(binaryLumini)LuminiString=morseToBinaryLumini(LuminiString);
			
			
			LuminiStrings[i] = LuminiString;
		}
	}
	
	public static void initLumLetters(String addBits, String zeichensatz) {
		for(int i=0; i<zeichensatz.length()&&i<256; i++) {
		LetterToLumini.put(zeichensatz.charAt(i), addBits+LuminiStrings[i]);
	}}

	public static String invertString(String string) {
		String invertString = "";

		for (int i = 0; i < string.length(); i++) {
			invertString = string.charAt(i) + invertString;
		}

		return invertString;
	}
	
	
	

	static {
		// 1. Array vor der Nutzung befüllen
		makeLuminiStrings(invertNumber);
		
		
		
		
		// neue Zeichensatz Steuerung ###
		initLumLetters("",zeichenfolge1);
		initLumLetters("",zeichenfolge2);
		initLumLetters("",zeichenfolge3);
		
//		

		// Leerzeichen
		LetterToLumini.put(' ', spaceSym2);

		// Umkehrabbildung
		for (Map.Entry<Character, String> entry : LetterToLumini.entrySet()) {
			LuminiToLetter.put(entry.getValue(), entry.getKey());
		}
	}

	// Text zu Lumini
	public static String toLumini(String text) {
		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
		for (char c : text.toCharArray()) {
			if (LetterToLumini.containsKey(c)) {
				sb.append(LetterToLumini.get(c)).append(spaceSym);
			}
		}
		String output =  sb.toString();
		output=output.trim();
		if(binaryLumini&&translatetyp==1)output=morseToBinary(output);
		if(binaryLumini&&translatetyp==2)output=morseToBinaryLumini2(output);
		return output;
	}

// Lumini -> Klartext
	public static String fromLumini(String morse) {
		StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
		String[] LuminiCodes = morse.split(spaceSym);
		for (String LuminiCode : LuminiCodes) {
			if (LuminiToLetter.containsKey(LuminiCode)) {
				sb.append(LuminiToLetter.get(LuminiCode));
			} else if (LuminiCode.equals(spaceSym)) {
				sb.append(" ");
			}
		}
		return sb.toString();
	}

			System.out.println("2 = LuminiCode → Text");

			System.out.println("5 = Level bzw. zu übersetzende randomwortZahl wählen");

			System.out.println("8 = boolean for new lumini, morse vs ascii, newLuminiNumbers vs numbers");
			System.out.println("9 = boolean for invert number");
			System.out.println("10 = ToText Wahrscheinlichkeit 0 bis 1 - Not implementet");
			System.out.println("11 = SpaceSims wählen");
			System.out.println("12 = ÜbersetzungZuVollkommenemBinärString");

			System.out.print("Wähle: ");

			int choice = scanner.nextInt();

			scanner.nextLine();

			switch (choice) {
			case 1:

			case 2:
				playLuminiToText(scanner);

			case 3:

			case 6:
			    System.out.print("Neue Basis (Zahl, z.B. 2 oder 10): ");
			    basis = scanner.nextInt();
			    reinitializeLuminiMappings(); // ❗ Füge diesen Aufruf hinzu
			    break;
			case 7:
			    System.out.print("Neuer Zeichensatz (String): ");
			    // Problem: Zeichensatz als String einzulesen ist kompliziert, da scanner.next() nur ein Token liest.
			    // Wenn Sie *luminiZeichen2* oder *MorseZeichen* verwenden möchten:

			    String newZeichensatzName = scanner.next();
			    // Beispielhafte Zuordnung (kann erweitert werden):
			    if ("luminiZeichen1".equalsIgnoreCase(newZeichensatzName)) {
			        zeichenfolge1 = luminiZeichen1;
			    } else if ("luminiZeichen2".equalsIgnoreCase(newZeichensatzName)) {
			        zeichenfolge1 = luminiZeichen2;
			    } else if ("MorseZeichen".equalsIgnoreCase(newZeichensatzName)) {
			        zeichenfolge1 = MorseZeichen;
			    } else {
			        // Falls ein eigener String eingegeben wird
			        zeichenfolge1 = newZeichensatzName;
			    }
			    // Setzen Sie zeichenfolge2 und zeichenfolge3 ebenfalls, falls gewünscht.
			    // zeichenfolge2 = zeichenfolge1;
			    // zeichenfolge3 = zeichenfolge1;

			    System.out.print("newLumini (true/false): ");
			    newLumini = scanner.nextBoolean();

			    break;
			case 9:
			    System.out.print("invertNumber (true/false): ");
			    invertNumber = scanner.nextBoolean();
			    reinitializeLuminiMappings(); // ❗ Füge diesen Aufruf hinzu
			    break;
